### Task C7: `/api/plans`

**Files:**
- Create: `swingbot/core/plan_store.py` (see the ground-truth deviation #1 at the top of this document — `PlanStore` does not exist anywhere in the repo yet, so this task writes it)
- Modify: `swingbot/admin/api.py`
- Test: `tests/admin/test_api.py`, `tests/core/test_plan_store.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `PlanStore().all(status=None) -> list[TradePlanV2]`, `.get(plan_id) -> TradePlanV2 | None`, `.update(plan) -> None`, backed by `data/plans.json` (a JSON array of `dataclasses.asdict(TradePlanV2)` dicts — same file-per-process-boundary convention as `trades.json`, re-read from disk on every call, never cached, for the same reason `TradeLog` isn't a singleton). `GET /api/plans?status=&tier=&badge=` → `{"plans": [...ranked plan dicts, each with "follow_score"...], "counts": {"PENDING": n, "ACTIVE": n, "PARTIAL": n, "CLOSED": n, "CANCELLED": n}}`, ranked via `analytics.rank.rank_plans`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test — `PlanStore` itself**

```python
# tests/core/test_plan_store.py
"""PlanStore -- data/plans.json backed store for TradePlanV2 records."""
import dataclasses

import pytest

from swingbot.core.plan_engine import PlanStatus, TradePlanV2


def _make_plan(plan_id="p1", ticker="AAPL", status=PlanStatus.PENDING) -> TradePlanV2:
    return TradePlanV2(
        plan_id=plan_id, ticker=ticker, created_at="2026-07-01", source="strategy",
        strategy="RSI", horizon_key="4w", direction="bullish", entry_type="market",
        trigger_price=100.0, entry_price=100.0, expiry_bars=5, stop_loss=95.0,
        tp1=104.0, tp1_fraction=0.5, tp2=110.0, breakeven_trigger_fraction=0.5,
        trail_atr_mult=2.5, quality_score=70, quality_breakdown=[], tier="A",
        badge="VALIDATED", badge_stats={}, status=status, status_history=[],
    )


@pytest.fixture
def store(tmp_path, monkeypatch):
    from swingbot import config
    from swingbot.core import plan_store
    monkeypatch.setattr(config, "DATA_DIR", str(tmp_path))
    return plan_store.PlanStore()


def test_update_then_get_roundtrips(store):
    plan = _make_plan()
    store.update(plan)
    fetched = store.get("p1")
    assert fetched is not None
    assert fetched.ticker == "AAPL"
    assert fetched.stop_loss == 95.0


def test_all_filters_by_status(store):
    store.update(_make_plan("p1", status=PlanStatus.PENDING))
    store.update(_make_plan("p2", status=PlanStatus.ACTIVE))
    assert len(store.all()) == 2
    assert [p.plan_id for p in store.all(status=PlanStatus.ACTIVE)] == ["p2"]


def test_update_overwrites_existing_by_plan_id(store):
    store.update(_make_plan("p1", status=PlanStatus.PENDING))
    plan = store.get("p1")
    plan.status = PlanStatus.ACTIVE
    store.update(plan)
    assert len(store.all()) == 1
    assert store.get("p1").status == PlanStatus.ACTIVE


def test_get_unknown_returns_none(store):
    assert store.get("does-not-exist") is None
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/core/test_plan_store.py -v`
Expected: FAIL — `ModuleNotFoundError: No module named 'swingbot.core.plan_store'`.

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement `swingbot/core/plan_store.py`**

```python
# swingbot/core/plan_store.py
"""JSON-backed store for TradePlanV2 records (data/plans.json).

Mirrors TradeLog's own "fresh read from disk every call, never a module
singleton" convention (see performance.py's TradeLog docstring) -- the
admin UI and the bot are separate processes sharing this one file, so a
cached copy in either process would go stale the moment the other writes.

NOTE (see this plan's ground-truth deviation #1): if Plan-engine-v2's own
live-plan-manager track lands a PlanStore first, delete this file and
import that one instead -- every call site in swingbot/admin/{api,pages}.py
uses exactly this interface (`all`, `get`, `update`), so nothing downstream
has to change either way.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import dataclasses
import json
import os

from swingbot import config
from swingbot.core.plan_engine import TradePlanV2


def _to_dict(plan: TradePlanV2) -> dict:
    return dataclasses.asdict(plan)


def _from_dict(d: dict) -> TradePlanV2:
    return TradePlanV2(**d)


class PlanStore:
    def _path(self) -> str:
        # Resolved at CALL time (not import/class-definition time) so tests
        # that monkeypatch config.DATA_DIR per-test are honored.
        return os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, "plans.json")

    def _read_all(self) -> list[dict]:
        path = self._path()
        if not os.path.exists(path):
            return []
        try:
            with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                return json.load(f)
        except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
            return []

    def _write_all(self, rows: list[dict]) -> None:
        path = self._path()
        os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
        with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump(rows, f, indent=2)

    def all(self, status: str | None = None) -> list[TradePlanV2]:
        plans = [_from_dict(d) for d in self._read_all()]
        if status is not None:
            plans = [p for p in plans if p.status == status]
        return plans

    def get(self, plan_id: str) -> TradePlanV2 | None:
        for p in self.all():
            if p.plan_id == plan_id:
                return p
        return None

    def update(self, plan: TradePlanV2) -> None:
        rows = self._read_all()
        for i, d in enumerate(rows):
            if d.get("plan_id") == plan.plan_id:
                rows[i] = _to_dict(plan)
                self._write_all(rows)
                return
        rows.append(_to_dict(plan))
        self._write_all(rows)
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Failing test — `/api/plans`**

```python
# tests/admin/test_api.py (append)
from swingbot.core.plan_engine import PlanStatus, TradePlanV2
from swingbot.core.plan_store import PlanStore


def _seed_plan(plan_id, ticker, status, tier="A", badge="VALIDATED"):
    plan = TradePlanV2(
        plan_id=plan_id, ticker=ticker, created_at="2026-07-01", source="strategy",
        strategy="RSI", horizon_key="4w", direction="bullish", entry_type="market",
        trigger_price=100.0, entry_price=100.0, expiry_bars=5, stop_loss=95.0,
        tp1=104.0, tp1_fraction=0.5, tp2=110.0, breakeven_trigger_fraction=0.5,
        trail_atr_mult=2.5, quality_score=70, quality_breakdown=[], tier=tier,
        badge=badge, badge_stats={}, status=status, status_history=[],
    )
    PlanStore().update(plan)
    return plan


def _fake_rank_plans(plans):
    """Deterministic stand-in for analytics.rank.rank_plans -- this test
    suite verifies API wiring/filtering/counts, not Plan A's real scoring
    formula (that's analytics' own test suite's job)."""
    rows = [dataclasses.asdict(p) for p in plans]
    for i, r in enumerate(sorted(rows, key=lambda r: r["plan_id"])):
        r["follow_score"] = 100 - i
    return sorted(rows, key=lambda r: -r["follow_score"])


import dataclasses  # noqa: E402 (kept near first use for readability in this test file)


def test_api_plans_ranked_and_counted(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.api.rank_plans", _fake_rank_plans)
    _seed_plan("p1", "AAPL", PlanStatus.PENDING)
    _seed_plan("p2", "MSFT", PlanStatus.ACTIVE)
    _seed_plan("p3", "TSLA", PlanStatus.ACTIVE, tier="B", badge="WEAK")

    r = client.get("/api/plans", headers=auth)
    body = r.get_json()
    assert [p["plan_id"] for p in body["plans"]] == ["p1", "p2", "p3"]  # follow_score descending
    assert body["counts"] == {"PENDING": 1, "ACTIVE": 2, "PARTIAL": 0, "CLOSED": 0, "CANCELLED": 0}


def test_api_plans_status_filter(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.api.rank_plans", _fake_rank_plans)
    _seed_plan("p1", "AAPL", PlanStatus.PENDING)
    _seed_plan("p2", "MSFT", PlanStatus.ACTIVE)
    r = client.get("/api/plans?status=ACTIVE", headers=auth)
    body = r.get_json()
    assert [p["plan_id"] for p in body["plans"]] == ["p2"]
    # Counts stay computed from the FULL set regardless of the row filter.
    assert body["counts"]["PENDING"] == 1
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_api.py -k api_plans -v`
Expected: FAIL — `404 NOT FOUND` (`/api/plans` doesn't exist yet).

- [ ] **Step 5: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/api.py -- add to the imports
from swingbot.analytics.rank import rank_plans
from swingbot.core.plan_engine import PlanStatus
from swingbot.core.plan_store import PlanStore

_ALL_PLAN_STATUSES = (
    PlanStatus.PENDING, PlanStatus.ACTIVE, PlanStatus.PARTIAL,
    PlanStatus.CLOSED, PlanStatus.CANCELLED,
)


def _plan_rows(status: str | None = None, tier: str | None = None,
               badge: str | None = None) -> dict:
    """Shared data-fetch for /api/plans (this task) and the Plans board
    page (extracted to pages.py and imported back here in Task C14, so
    both surfaces slice identically per the plan's Global Constraints).
    Counts are always computed from the UNFILTERED set -- the lifecycle
    strip (C15) must show the true per-status totals no matter which
    status/tier/badge filter is currently applied to the row list."""
    all_plans = PlanStore().all(status=None)
    counts = {s: 0 for s in _ALL_PLAN_STATUSES}
    for p in all_plans:
        counts[p.status] = counts.get(p.status, 0) + 1

    rows = rank_plans(all_plans)  # each row: plan fields + "follow_score"
    if status:
        rows = [r for r in rows if r["status"] == status]
    if tier:
        rows = [r for r in rows if r["tier"] == tier]
    if badge:
        rows = [r for r in rows if r["badge"] == badge]
    return {"plans": rows, "counts": counts}


@api.route("/plans", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth_json
def api_plans():
    return jsonify(_plan_rows(
        status=request.args.get("status") or None,
        tier=request.args.get("tier") or None,
        badge=request.args.get("badge") or None,
    ))
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_api.py tests/core/test_plan_store.py -v` → all green.

```bash
git commit -m "feat: /api/plans"
```

### Task C8: `/api/journal`

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/api.py`; test `tests/admin/test_api.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `GET /api/journal?strategy=&tag=&outcome=&has_note=&limit=100` → `{"entries": [...]}` via `analytics.journal.JournalStore().entries(...)`; `POST /api/journal/<trade_id>/note` (form field OR JSON body key `note`) → `{"ok": true}`, or `{"ok": false}` with **404** for an unknown `trade_id`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_api.py (append)

class _FakeJournalStore:
    _ENTRIES = [
        {"trade_id": "t1", "ticker": "AAPL", "strategy": "RSI", "tags": ["clean_breakout"], "outcome": "win", "note": None},
        {"trade_id": "t2", "ticker": "MSFT", "strategy": "MACD", "tags": ["chased"], "outcome": "loss", "note": "entered late"},
    ]

    def entries(self, strategy=None, tag=None, outcome=None, has_note=None, limit=100):
        rows = list(self._ENTRIES)
        if strategy:
            rows = [r for r in rows if r["strategy"] == strategy]
        if tag:
            rows = [r for r in rows if tag in r["tags"]]
        if outcome:
            rows = [r for r in rows if r["outcome"] == outcome]
        if has_note is not None:
            rows = [r for r in rows if (r["note"] is not None) == has_note]
        return rows[:limit]

    def set_note(self, trade_id, note):
        for r in self._ENTRIES:
            if r["trade_id"] == trade_id:
                r["note"] = note
                return True
        return False


def test_api_journal_filters_by_tag(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.api.JournalStore", _FakeJournalStore)
    r = client.get("/api/journal?tag=chased", headers=auth)
    body = r.get_json()
    assert [e["trade_id"] for e in body["entries"]] == ["t2"]


def test_api_journal_note_roundtrips(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.api.JournalStore", _FakeJournalStore)
    r = client.post("/api/journal/t1/note", data={"note": "good clean entry"}, headers=auth)
    assert r.get_json() == {"ok": True}


def test_api_journal_note_unknown_id_404(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.api.JournalStore", _FakeJournalStore)
    r = client.post("/api/journal/does-not-exist/note", data={"note": "x"}, headers=auth)
    assert r.status_code == 404
    assert r.get_json() == {"ok": False}
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/api.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.analytics.journal import JournalStore


def _parse_bool_param(v: str | None) -> bool | None:
    if v is None or v == "":
        return None
    return v.lower() in ("1", "true", "yes")


@api.route("/journal", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth_json
def api_journal():
    store = JournalStore()
    entries = store.entries(
        strategy=request.args.get("strategy") or None,
        tag=request.args.get("tag") or None,
        outcome=request.args.get("outcome") or None,
        has_note=_parse_bool_param(request.args.get("has_note")),
        limit=int(request.args.get("limit", 100)),
    )
    return jsonify({"entries": entries})


@api.route("/journal/<trade_id>/note", methods=["POST"])
@require_auth_json
def api_journal_note(trade_id):
    payload = request.get_json(silent=True) or {}
    note = request.form.get("note", payload.get("note", ""))
    ok = JournalStore().set_note(trade_id, note)
    if not ok:
        return jsonify({"ok": False}), 404
    return jsonify({"ok": True})
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/api.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.core.registry import load_registry


@api.route("/calibration", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth_json
def api_calibration():
    snap = load_snapshot(max_age_seconds=3600) or refresh_snapshot()
    calibration = snap.get("calibration", {}) if snap else {}
    return jsonify({
        "deciles": calibration.get("deciles", []),
        "tiers": calibration.get("tiers", []),
        "drift": calibration.get("drift", []),
    })


@api.route("/registry", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth_json
def api_registry():
    snap = load_snapshot(max_age_seconds=3600) or refresh_snapshot()
    by_strategy = ((snap or {}).get("by") or {}).get("strategy", {})
    rows = []
    for rec in load_registry():
        live = by_strategy.get(rec["strategy"], {})
        rows.append({**rec, "live_n": live.get("n"), "live_wr": live.get("win_rate")})
    return jsonify({"registry": rows})
```

### Task C10: ETag on the dashboard fragment

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/app.py` (`dashboard_fragment` route, line 604), `swingbot/admin/templates/dashboard.html` (`refreshDashboard()`, lines 128–138); test `tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `/dashboard/fragment` computes `sha1(html)` → `ETag`; a request with a matching `If-None-Match` → `304` with an empty body. `dashboard.html`'s `refreshDashboard()` sends the previously-received ETag on every subsequent poll and, on `304`, skips the morphdom patch entirely (leaves the DOM untouched — nothing changed).

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py
"""Response-header behaviors: ETag/304 polling, gzip, chart caching."""


def test_dashboard_fragment_etag_304(client, auth):
    r1 = client.get("/dashboard/fragment", headers=auth)
    assert r1.status_code == 200
    etag = r1.headers.get("ETag")
    assert etag, "expected an ETag header on the fragment response"

    r2 = client.get("/dashboard/fragment", headers={**auth, "If-None-Match": etag})
    assert r2.status_code == 304
    assert r2.data == b""


def test_dashboard_fragment_etag_changes_when_content_changes(client, auth):
    r1 = client.get("/dashboard/fragment?mode=all", headers=auth)
    r2 = client.get("/dashboard/fragment?mode=today", headers=auth)
    # Different query params -> (usually) different rendered HTML -> different ETag.
    # Both still 200 since neither request sent an If-None-Match at all.
    assert r1.status_code == 200 and r2.status_code == 200
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py -v`
Expected: FAIL — `assert etag` fails (`ETag` header not present yet).

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the route (`app.py`, replacing the current `dashboard_fragment` view at line 604)**

```python
# swingbot/admin/app.py -- add near the top imports
import hashlib
```

```python
@app.route("/dashboard/fragment", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def dashboard_fragment():
    """
    Just the open-trades table + stats, re-rendered fresh from
    trades.json. Polled by the dashboard's own JS every few seconds so a
    trade logged by `!check` (or the background scan) shows up without
    a manual browser refresh -- the admin process is separate from the
    bot process, so nothing pushes it a notification; it has to ask.

    ETag'd on the rendered HTML's sha1: when nothing has actually changed
    since the browser's last poll (the common case -- most 5s ticks see
    no new trade), the response is a 5-byte "304 Not Modified" instead of
    the full fragment, which on a page auto-refreshing indefinitely adds
    up to a meaningful bandwidth/CPU (Jinja render) saving over a session.
    """
    html = _render_dashboard_fragment()
    etag = hashlib.sha1(html.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
    if request.headers.get("If-None-Match") == etag:
        return Response(status=304)
    resp = Response(html, mimetype="text/html; charset=utf-8")
    resp.headers["ETag"] = etag
    return resp
```

- [ ] **Step 3: Update `dashboard.html`'s `refreshDashboard()` (lines 128–138 in the current file)**

```diff
+  var _lastFragmentEtag = null;
   function refreshDashboard() {
-    fetch('{{ url_for("dashboard_fragment") }}?mode=' + encodeURIComponent(dashboardMode), { credentials: 'include' })
+    var _pollHeaders = {};
+    if (_lastFragmentEtag) { _pollHeaders['If-None-Match'] = _lastFragmentEtag; }
+    fetch('{{ url_for("dashboard_fragment") }}?mode=' + encodeURIComponent(dashboardMode),
+          { credentials: 'include', headers: _pollHeaders })
       .then(function(r) {
         if (r.status === 401) {
           window.location.reload();
           return null;
         }
+        if (r.status === 304) { return undefined; } // unchanged since last poll -- nothing to patch
+        _lastFragmentEtag = r.headers.get('ETag');
         return r.text();
       })
       .then(function(html) {
+        if (html === undefined) {
+          document.getElementById('refresh-status').textContent = 'Up to date ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
+          return;
+        }
         if (!html) return;
         var container = document.getElementById('dashboard-fragment');
```

- [ ] **Step 4: PASS**

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py -v` → 2 passed.

### Task C11: gzip responses

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/app.py` (new `after_request` hook, placed right after the logging setup block, i.e. after line 109 and before `_berlin_time`'s definition); test `tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: a hand-rolled `@app.after_request` gzip hook for `text/html`/`application/json` bodies over 4 KB, only when the client sends `Accept-Encoding: gzip`, skipping anything already encoded or `direct_passthrough` (i.e. `send_file` responses — chart PNGs, CSV export — are never touched, both because they're usually already-compressed binary and because mutating a passthrough response's body breaks streaming). No `flask-compress` dependency.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python

    assert b"Dashboard" in gzip.decompress(r.data)

    assert r.headers.get("Content-Encoding") is None
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py -k gzip -v`

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/app.py -- add near the top imports
import gzip
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/app.py -- placed right after the admin-log-handler setup
# block (after line 109), before _berlin_time's definition.
@app.after_request
def _gzip_response(response):
    """Hand-rolled response gzip -- no flask-compress dependency (the plan's
    "no new pip dependencies" constraint). Only compresses text/html and
    application/json bodies over 4 KB when the client advertises gzip
    support; send_file responses (chart PNGs, CSV export) are always
    direct_passthrough and are left completely alone, both because they're
    usually already-compressed binary and because rewriting a passthrough
    response's body would break Flask's streaming path."""
    accept_encoding = request.headers.get("Accept-Encoding", "")
    if "gzip" not in accept_encoding:
        return response
    if response.direct_passthrough or response.content_encoding:
        return response
    if response.mimetype not in ("text/html", "application/json"):
        return response
    body = response.get_data()
    if len(body) < 4096:
        return response
    compressed = gzip.compress(body, compresslevel=6)
    response.set_data(compressed)
    response.headers["Content-Encoding"] = "gzip"
    response.headers["Content-Length"] = str(len(compressed))
    response.headers.add("Vary", "Accept-Encoding")
    return response
```

- [ ] **Step 3: PASS, Step 4: Commit**

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py -k gzip -v` → 3 passed.

```bash
git add swingbot/admin/app.py tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py
git commit -m "perf: gzip admin responses"
```

### Task C12: Chart image caching

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/app.py` (`trade_chart_image`, line 768); test `tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: closed-trade chart responses get `Cache-Control: private, max-age=86400` + `Last-Modified`, honoring `If-Modified-Since` with a `304`; open-trade chart responses get `Cache-Control: no-store` (an open trade's chart is never stable — price/levels can change on every refresh). No dependency on Plan B's `charts/cache.py` (per the abbreviated plan's fallback note) — this task's version is self-contained.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python

import os

_TINY_PNG = bytes.fromhex(
    "89504e470d0a1a0a0000000d4948445200000001000000010802000000907753"
    "de0000000c4944415478da6360606060000000050001d78f7e6e0000000049454e44ae426082"
)


def _seed_trade(config_data_dir, trade_id, status, closed_at=None):
    path = os.path.join(config_data_dir, "trades.json")
    trades = json.load(open(path)) if os.path.exists(path) else []
    trades.append({
        "id": trade_id, "ticker": "AAPL", "status": status, "direction": "bullish",
        "entry": 100.0, "stop_loss": 95.0, "take_profit": 110.0,
        "opened_at": "2026-01-01T00:00:00+00:00", "closed_at": closed_at,
        "confidence_level": 3, "confidence_score": 60, "strategy": "RSI", "horizon_key": "4w",
    })
    json.dump(trades, open(path, "w"))


def test_closed_trade_chart_is_cacheable(client, auth, admin_app, tmp_path, monkeypatch):

    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.app.regenerate_chart_for_trade", lambda t: str(png_path))

    r = client.get("/trades/t1/chart.png", headers=auth)

    assert r.headers.get("Cache-Control") == "private, max-age=86400"
    assert r.headers.get("Last-Modified")

```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py -k chart -v`
Expected: FAIL — `assert r.headers.get("Cache-Control") == "private, max-age=86400"` (no such header yet — `None`).

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement (replacing the current `trade_chart_image` view at line 768)**

```python
@app.route("/trades/<trade_id>/chart.png", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def trade_chart_image(trade_id):
    t = _trades().get_trade_by_id(trade_id)
    if not t:
        abort(404)
    path = regenerate_chart_for_trade(t)
    if not path:
        abort(404, "Could not generate a chart for this trade right now (data fetch may have failed).")

    resp = send_file(path, mimetype="image/png")
    if t["status"] == "open":
        # An open trade's chart can change on every single refresh (price
        # moves, new bars) -- never let the browser reuse a stale copy.
        resp.headers["Cache-Control"] = "no-store"
        return resp

    # Closed trades are deterministic -- the same trade_id always
    # regenerates the identical chart (entry/stop/target/outcome are all
    # frozen), so it's safe to let the browser cache it for a day and skip
    # regenerating the image (a real matplotlib render, not free) on every
    # repeat view of the same trade's detail page.
    resp.headers["Cache-Control"] = "private, max-age=86400"
    try:
        mtime = os.path.getmtime(path)
        last_modified = datetime.fromtimestamp(mtime, tz=timezone.utc)
        resp.headers["Last-Modified"] = last_modified.strftime("%a, %d %b %Y %H:%M:%S GMT")
        ims = request.headers.get("If-Modified-Since")
        if ims:
            ims_dt = datetime.strptime(ims, "%a, %d %b %Y %H:%M:%S GMT").replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
            if last_modified <= ims_dt:
                return Response(status=304)
    except (OSError, ValueError):
        pass
    return resp
```

- [ ] **Step 3: PASS, Step 4: Commit**

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py -k chart -v` → 2 passed.

```bash
git add swingbot/admin/app.py tests/admin/test_perf_headers.py
git commit -m "perf: chart.png cache headers"
```

### Task C13: Server-side history pagination

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/app.py` (`_render_dashboard_fragment`, closed-trades section around lines 349–354), `swingbot/admin/templates/dashboard_fragment.html` (Trade History card header, around line 588)
- Test: `tests/admin/test_dashboard_v2.py`

**⚠️ Deviation from the abbreviated plan:** the current `_render_dashboard_fragment` already caps the rendered closed-trades table at a hard **25** rows (`closed_trades = sorted(all_closed_trades, ...)[:25]`), not the "renders everything, paginates client-side up to whatever N" the abbreviated task's "when closed trades > 500" framing implied. That 25-row cap already makes the Trade History table's own per-page selector (10/25/50/**All**) partly non-functional — picking "50 per page" or "All" today can never show more than the 25 rows the server ever sent. This task resolves that by raising the server-side cap to **500** (bounding the payload as the abbreviated plan intended) and adding the truncation banner once the *true* full history exceeds it — which also, as a side effect, makes the existing 50/All per-page options actually mean something for the first time.

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: when total closed-trade count > 500, the fragment renders only the newest 500 with a banner *"Showing latest 500 of N closed trades — use the Performance page or export for full history"*; the existing client-side filter/sort/pagination JS (`ct-*` in `dashboard_fragment.html`) is untouched and now has up to 500 real rows to actually paginate through instead of a fixed 25.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
            "entry": 100.0, "stop_loss": 95.0, "take_profit": 110.0, "exit_price": 110.0,
            "opened_at": "2026-01-01T00:00:00+00:00",
            "closed_at": f"2026-{(i % 12) + 1:02d}-{(i % 28) + 1:02d}T00:00:00+00:00",
            "confidence_level": 3, "confidence_score": 60, "strategy": "RSI", "horizon_key": "4w",
        })
    with open(os.path.join(data_dir, "trades.json"), "w") as f:
```

# Phase C2 — Plans board (Tasks C14–C19)

### Task C14: Plans page

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/pages.py`, `swingbot/admin/api.py` (remove the now-duplicated `_plan_rows`, import it from `pages.py` instead); create `swingbot/admin/templates/_plans_board.html`; rewrite `swingbot/admin/templates/plans.html`; test `tests/admin/test_pages.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `/plans` renders the board server-side from `_plan_rows` (moved here from `api.py`, which now imports it back — "extract `_plan_rows(status, tier, badge) -> dict` shared by page and API" per the plan brief). Table columns: ⭐ tier/badge chips · ticker · direction · status · follow score · entry/trigger · SL · TP1 · TP2 · age · quality. Rows will link to `/plans/<plan_id>` once that route exists (Task C19 wires the `onclick`; this task leaves rows non-clickable to avoid a `BuildError` on an endpoint that doesn't exist yet).
- This task also establishes the dashboard's own split pattern (`_render_dashboard_fragment()` / `render_template("dashboard_fragment.html", ...)` / `{{ fragment | safe }}`) for the Plans board from day one: `_render_plans_board(rows, counts, filters) -> str` renders just the `_plans_board.html` partial, and `plans_page()` embeds that HTML string into the full `plans.html` page — so Task C18's auto-refresh route is a pure addition (a thin route wrapping the same helper), not a rewrite.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_pages.py (append)
import dataclasses

from swingbot.core.plan_engine import PlanStatus, TradePlanV2
from swingbot.core.plan_store import PlanStore


def _plan(plan_id, ticker, tier="A", badge="VALIDATED", status=PlanStatus.PENDING):
    return TradePlanV2(
        plan_id=plan_id, ticker=ticker, created_at="2026-07-01", source="strategy",
        strategy="RSI", horizon_key="4w", direction="bullish", entry_type="market",
        trigger_price=100.0, entry_price=100.0, expiry_bars=5, stop_loss=95.0,
        tp1=104.0, tp1_fraction=0.5, tp2=110.0, breakeven_trigger_fraction=0.5,
        trail_atr_mult=2.5, quality_score=70, quality_breakdown=[], tier=tier,
        badge=badge, badge_stats={}, status=status, status_history=[],
    )


def _fake_rank_plans_by_ticker(plans):
    rows = [dataclasses.asdict(p) for p in plans]
    for r in rows:
        r["follow_score"] = 100.0
    return sorted(rows, key=lambda r: r["ticker"])


def test_plans_page_renders_ranked_rows_with_chips(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    PlanStore().update(_plan("p1", "MSFT", tier="A", badge="VALIDATED"))
    PlanStore().update(_plan("p2", "AAPL", tier="B", badge="WEAK"))
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.pages.rank_plans", _fake_rank_plans_by_ticker)

    r = client.get("/plans", headers=auth)
    html = r.data.decode("utf-8")
    assert "chip-tier-a" in html
    assert "chip-validated" in html
    assert html.index("AAPL") < html.index("MSFT")  # ranked order = alphabetical per the fake
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_pages.py -k plans_page -v`
Expected: FAIL — `assert "chip-tier-a" in html` (still the C5 empty-state shell).

- [ ] **Step 4: Implement `pages.py`, remove the duplicate from `api.py`**

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from flask import render_template, request

from swingbot.analytics.rank import rank_plans
from swingbot.core.plan_engine import PlanStatus
from swingbot.core.plan_store import PlanStore

_ALL_PLAN_STATUSES = (
    PlanStatus.PENDING, PlanStatus.ACTIVE, PlanStatus.PARTIAL,
    PlanStatus.CLOSED, PlanStatus.CANCELLED,
)


def _plan_rows(status: str | None = None, tier: str | None = None,
               badge: str | None = None) -> dict:
    """Shared by the Plans board page (this task) and /api/plans (C7 --
    api.py now imports this function instead of keeping its own copy).
    Counts are always computed from the UNFILTERED set (Task C15 refines
    this further to scope CLOSED/CANCELLED counts to "today")."""
    all_plans = PlanStore().all(status=None)
    counts = {s: 0 for s in _ALL_PLAN_STATUSES}
    for p in all_plans:
        counts[p.status] = counts.get(p.status, 0) + 1

    rows = rank_plans(all_plans)
    if status:
        rows = [r for r in rows if r["status"] == status]
    if tier:
        rows = [r for r in rows if r["tier"] == tier]
    if badge:
        rows = [r for r in rows if r["badge"] == badge]
    return {"plans": rows, "counts": counts}


def _render_plans_board(rows: list, counts: dict, filters: dict) -> str:
    return render_template("_plans_board.html", plans=rows, counts=counts, filters=filters)


@pages.route("/plans", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def plans_page():
    filters = {
        "status": request.args.get("status", ""),
        "tier": request.args.get("tier", ""),
        "badge": request.args.get("badge", ""),
    }
    result = _plan_rows(status=filters["status"] or None, tier=filters["tier"] or None,
                        badge=filters["badge"] or None)
    fragment = _render_plans_board(result["plans"], result["counts"], filters)
    return _render("Plans", "plans", "plans.html", fragment=fragment)
```

Replace the old `plans_page()` shell from Task C5 with this one (same function name, same route).

```diff
 # swingbot/admin/api.py

-from swingbot.core.plan_store import PlanStore
-
-_ALL_PLAN_STATUSES = (...)
-
-def _plan_rows(status=None, tier=None, badge=None) -> dict:
-    ...
+from .pages import _plan_rows
```

### Task C15: Lifecycle strip

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/templates/_plans_board.html`, `swingbot/admin/pages.py`; test `tests/admin/test_pages.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: a `.lifecycle-strip` card row above the board — one card per status: PENDING / ACTIVE / PARTIAL / **CLOSED-today** / **CANCELLED-today** (the last two scoped to today's Europe/Berlin calendar day — an all-time CLOSED/CANCELLED count only grows and stops being a useful "what needs attention" signal, whereas PENDING/ACTIVE/PARTIAL are naturally small since plans leave those states). Clicking a card applies that status filter via `?status=`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_pages.py (append)
from datetime import datetime, timezone


def test_lifecycle_strip_counts_and_click_filters(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.pages.rank_plans", lambda plans: [
        {**dataclasses.asdict(p), "follow_score": 1.0} for p in plans
    ])
    PlanStore().update(_plan("p1", "AAPL", status=PlanStatus.PENDING))
    PlanStore().update(_plan("p2", "MSFT", status=PlanStatus.ACTIVE))
    today_closed = _plan("p3", "TSLA", status=PlanStatus.CLOSED)
    today_closed.status_history = [{"status": "CLOSED", "reason": "manual",
                                    "at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}]
    PlanStore().update(today_closed)

    r = client.get("/plans", headers=auth)
    html = r.data.decode("utf-8")
    assert 'href="/plans?status=PENDING' in html
    assert ">1<" in html  # PENDING count of 1 shows somewhere in the strip

    r2 = client.get("/plans?status=PENDING", headers=auth)
    html2 = r2.data.decode("utf-8")
    assert "AAPL" in html2 and "MSFT" not in html2
```

```diff
 def _plan_rows(status: str | None = None, tier: str | None = None,
                badge: str | None = None) -> dict:
     all_plans = PlanStore().all(status=None)
     counts = {s: 0 for s in _ALL_PLAN_STATUSES}
     for p in all_plans:
-        counts[p.status] = counts.get(p.status, 0) + 1
+        if p.status in (PlanStatus.CLOSED, PlanStatus.CANCELLED):
+            last_at = p.status_history[-1]["at"] if p.status_history else None
```

### Task C17: Plan actions (cancel / close)

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/pages.py`, `swingbot/admin/templates/_plans_board.html`; test `tests/admin/test_pages.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `POST /plans/<plan_id>/cancel` — PENDING only: `record_transition(plan, PlanStatus.CANCELLED, reason="manual")` + `PlanStore.update`, then queues the existing `manual_close_notify.json` mechanism (same file `app.py`'s `close_trade_manual` already writes to) so the bot posts the transition to Discord; **400** if the plan isn't PENDING. `POST /plans/<plan_id>/close` — ACTIVE/PARTIAL only: also closes the linked trade (if any, via `TradeLog.close_trade_manual`) the same way the dashboard's own "✕ close trade" button does; **400** if the plan isn't ACTIVE/PARTIAL. Confirm dialogs in the template (`onsubmit="return confirm(...)"`, matching the existing dashboard buttons' pattern).

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_pages.py (append)
import os


def test_cancel_pending_plan_transitions_and_notifies(client, auth):
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_pages.py -k "cancel_ or close_" -v`
Expected: FAIL — `404 NOT FOUND` (routes don't exist).

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
import dataclasses
import json
import os

from flask import abort, redirect, url_for

from swingbot.core.performance import TradeLog
from swingbot.core.plan_engine import record_transition

from .app import MANUAL_CLOSE_QUEUE


def _queue_manual_close_notify(plan) -> None:
    """Same file app.py's close_trade route already appends to (see
    MANUAL_CLOSE_QUEUE's module docstring in app.py) -- the bot's own poll
    loop picks this up and posts the transition to Discord. A plan-level
    entry is tagged "kind": "plan_transition" so the bot's consumer can
    format it distinctly from a raw trade-close entry."""
    try:
        existing = []
        if os.path.exists(MANUAL_CLOSE_QUEUE):
            with open(MANUAL_CLOSE_QUEUE, "r") as f:
                existing = json.load(f)
        existing.append({"kind": "plan_transition", **dataclasses.asdict(plan)})
        with open(MANUAL_CLOSE_QUEUE, "w") as f:
            json.dump(existing, f)
    except Exception:
        pass  # best-effort notify -- never block the actual state transition on this


@pages.route("/plans/<plan_id>/cancel", methods=["POST"])
@require_auth
def plan_cancel(plan_id):
    store = PlanStore()
    plan = store.get(plan_id)
    if not plan:
        abort(404, f"No plan found with id '{plan_id}'.")
    if plan.status != PlanStatus.PENDING:
        abort(400, "Only PENDING plans can be cancelled.")
    record_transition(plan, PlanStatus.CANCELLED, reason="manual")
    store.update(plan)
    _queue_manual_close_notify(plan)
    return redirect(url_for("pages.plans_page", msg=f"Plan {plan.ticker} cancelled.", ok=1))


@pages.route("/plans/<plan_id>/close", methods=["POST"])
@require_auth
def plan_close(plan_id):
    store = PlanStore()
    plan = store.get(plan_id)
    if not plan:
        abort(404, f"No plan found with id '{plan_id}'.")
    if plan.status not in (PlanStatus.ACTIVE, PlanStatus.PARTIAL):
        abort(400, "Only ACTIVE/PARTIAL plans can be closed.")
    tl = TradeLog()
    linked = next((t for t in tl.get_trades(status=None, limit=None) if t.get("plan_id") == plan_id), None)
    if linked and linked["status"] == "open":
        tl.close_trade_manual(linked["id"], reason="manual (plan close, admin UI)")
    record_transition(plan, PlanStatus.CLOSED, reason="manual")
    store.update(plan)
    _queue_manual_close_notify(plan)
    return redirect(url_for("pages.plans_page", msg=f"Plan {plan.ticker} closed.", ok=1))
```

```jinja
{# swingbot/admin/templates/_plans_board.html -- add an Action column: #}
```
```diff
       <th>Age</th>
       <th>Quality</th>
+      <th>Action</th>
     </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
     {% for p in plans %}
     <tr>
       ...
       <td>{{ p.quality_score }}</td>
+      <td onclick="event.stopPropagation();">
+        {% if p.status == 'PENDING' %}
+        <form method="post" action="{{ url_for('pages.plan_cancel', plan_id=p.plan_id) }}" style="margin:0;display:inline;"
+              onsubmit="return confirm('Cancel plan for {{ p.ticker }}?');">
+          <button type="submit" class="icon-btn danger" title="Cancel plan">✕</button>
+        </form>
+        {% elif p.status in ('ACTIVE', 'PARTIAL') %}
+        <form method="post" action="{{ url_for('pages.plan_close', plan_id=p.plan_id) }}" style="margin:0;display:inline;"
+              onsubmit="return confirm('Close plan for {{ p.ticker }}?');">
+          <button type="submit" class="icon-btn danger" title="Close plan">✕</button>
+        </form>
+        {% else %}
+        <span class="muted">—</span>
+        {% endif %}
+      </td>
     </tr>
     {% endfor %}
```

- [ ] **Step 3: PASS, Step 4: Commit**

### Task C18: Board auto-refresh

```python
def test_plans_fragment_etag_304(client, auth):
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
import hashlib

from flask import Response
```

```python
@pages.route("/plans/fragment", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def plans_fragment():
    filters = {
        "status": request.args.get("status", ""),
        "tier": request.args.get("tier", ""),
        "badge": request.args.get("badge", ""),
        "ticker": request.args.get("ticker", ""),
    }
    result = _plan_rows(status=filters["status"] or None, tier=filters["tier"] or None,
                        badge=filters["badge"] or None, ticker=filters["ticker"] or None)
    html = _render_plans_board(result["plans"], result["counts"], filters)
    etag = hashlib.sha1(html.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
    if request.headers.get("If-None-Match") == etag:
        return Response(status=304)
    resp = Response(html, mimetype="text/html; charset=utf-8")
    resp.headers["ETag"] = etag
    return resp
```

Also update `plans_page()` to accept `ticker` (Task C16 already added it to `filters`, but the fragment route above duplicates that filter-dict construction — both are kept in sync since they call the same `_plan_rows`).

```jinja
{# swingbot/admin/templates/plans.html -- full replacement #}
{% extends "base.html" %}
{% block body %}
<div id="plans-fragment">{{ fragment | safe }}</div>
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='vendor/morphdom-umd.min.js') }}"></script>
<script>
(function () {
  var _lastEtag = null;
  function refreshPlansBoard() {
    var qs = new URL(window.location.href).search;  // preserve current filter params
    var headers = {};
    if (_lastEtag) { headers['If-None-Match'] = _lastEtag; }
    fetch('{{ url_for("pages.plans_fragment") }}' + qs, { credentials: 'include', headers: headers })
      .then(function (r) {
        if (r.status === 401) { window.location.reload(); return null; }
        if (r.status === 304) { return undefined; }
        _lastEtag = r.headers.get('ETag');
        return r.text();
      })
      .then(function (html) {
        if (html === undefined || !html) return;
        var container = document.getElementById('plans-fragment');
        if (typeof morphdom !== 'undefined') {
          var wrapper = document.createElement('div');
          wrapper.id = 'plans-fragment';
          wrapper.innerHTML = html;
          morphdom(container, wrapper);
        } else {
          container.innerHTML = html;
        }
      })
      .catch(function () {});
  }
  setInterval(refreshPlansBoard, {{ (dashboard_refresh_seconds * 1000) | int }});
})();
</script>
{% endblock %}
```

```diff

 @pages.route("/plans", methods=["GET"])

 def plans_page():
     ...
     fragment = _render_plans_board(result["plans"], result["counts"], filters)
-    return _render("Plans", "plans", "plans.html", fragment=fragment)
+    return _render("Plans", "plans", "plans.html", fragment=fragment,
+                   dashboard_refresh_seconds=config.DASHBOARD_REFRESH_SECONDS)
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.core.charts.trade_chart import generate_trade_chart
from swingbot.core.data import get_daily_data
from swingbot.core.strategy_types import HORIZONS


@pages.route("/plans/<plan_id>", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def plan_detail_page(plan_id):
    plan = PlanStore().get(plan_id)
    if not plan:
        abort(404, f"No plan found with id '{plan_id}'.")

    tl = TradeLog()
    linked_trade = next(
        (t for t in tl.get_trades(status=None, limit=None) if t.get("plan_id") == plan_id), None,
    )

    # analytics.rank may or may not expose a per-plan breakdown function
    # depending on how far Plan A's own scope went -- fall back to the
    # score alone (already shown in badge_stats/quality_score) rather than
    # failing the whole page over an optional enrichment.
    follow_breakdown = None
    try:
        from swingbot.analytics.rank import follow_breakdown as _follow_breakdown
        follow_breakdown = _follow_breakdown(plan)
    except (ImportError, AttributeError):
        follow_breakdown = None

    return _render(
        f"{plan.ticker} — Plan {plan.plan_id[:8]}", "plans", "plan_detail.html",
        plan=plan, linked_trade=linked_trade, follow_breakdown=follow_breakdown,
    )


@pages.route("/plans/<plan_id>/chart.png", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def plan_chart_image(plan_id):
    plan = PlanStore().get(plan_id)
    if not plan:
        abort(404)
    df = get_daily_data(plan.ticker)
    if df is None:
        abort(404, "Could not fetch chart data for this plan right now (data fetch may have failed).")
    h = HORIZONS.get(plan.horizon_key, {})
    path = generate_trade_chart(
        plan.ticker, df,
        entry=plan.entry_price or plan.trigger_price,
        stop_loss=plan.stop_loss, take_profit=plan.tp1,
        direction=plan.direction, strategy=plan.strategy,
        horizon_label=h.get("label", plan.horizon_key),
    )
    return send_file(path, mimetype="image/png")
```

`send_file` must be imported into `pages.py` from `flask` alongside the other Flask imports already there.

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.analytics.snapshots import load_snapshot, refresh_snapshot
from swingbot.core.registry import load_registry
from swingbot.core.strategy_types import STRATEGY_GATES, STRATEGY_RR_OVERRIDE


def _gate_description(strategy: str) -> str:
    """Human-readable rendering of a STRATEGY_GATES entry -- e.g.
    Fibonacci's real current {"directions": ("bullish",)} becomes
    "bullish only"; VWAP's {"directions": ("bullish",),
    "horizons": ("4w","6m","7m","8m","9m")} becomes
    "bullish only {4w,6m,7m,8m,9m}". A missing key means no gate at all
    (both directions, every horizon)."""
    gate = STRATEGY_GATES.get(strategy)
    if not gate:
        return "no gate (all directions, all horizons)"
    parts = []
    directions = gate.get("directions")
    if directions:
        parts.append(f"{'/'.join(directions)} only" if len(directions) == 1 else "/".join(directions))
    horizons = gate.get("horizons")
    if horizons:
        parts.append("{" + ",".join(horizons) + "}")
    return " ".join(parts) if parts else "no gate (all directions, all horizons)"


def _registry_rows() -> list[dict]:
    """Shared by /strategies (this task) and /api/registry (C9 -- api.py
    now imports this instead of keeping its own copy). ASSUMED SHAPE:
    the snapshot's "by.strategy" maps strategy name -> {"n", "win_rate"}
    (confirmed by the task brief's own phrasing); confirm against Plan A's
    real implementation at merge."""
    snap = load_snapshot(max_age_seconds=3600) or refresh_snapshot()
    by_strategy = ((snap or {}).get("by") or {}).get("strategy", {})
    rows = []
    for rec in load_registry():
        live = by_strategy.get(rec["strategy"], {})
        rows.append({
            **rec,
            "live_n": live.get("n"),
            "live_wr": live.get("win_rate"),
            "rr_override": STRATEGY_RR_OVERRIDE.get(rec["strategy"]),
            "gate_description": _gate_description(rec["strategy"]),
        })
    return rows


@pages.route("/strategies", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def strategies_page():
    return _render("Strategies", "strategies", "strategies.html", rows=_registry_rows())
```

```diff
-        live = by_strategy.get(rec["strategy"], {})
-        rows.append({**rec, "live_n": live.get("n"), "live_wr": live.get("win_rate")})
-    return jsonify({"registry": rows})
+    return jsonify({"registry": _registry_rows()})
```

```jinja
      out-of-sample validation status per strategy
    </span>
  </p>
```

### Task C21: Strategy × horizon heatmap

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/templates/strategies.html`, `swingbot/admin/pages.py`; test `tests/admin/test_pages.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: a `.heatmap-grid` of live win-rate per (strategy, horizon), computed via `analytics.aggregate.stats_by` on the closed-trade list — **the one place per this plan's Global Constraints a route calls an analytics function directly** (a live aggregation over trades, still zero win-rate/expectancy *formulas* written in the route or template — `stats_by` does the actual math). Cell color: linear red (≤60) → amber (75) → green (≥85); cell text `WR% (n)`; `n < 5` cells render greyed `n/a`.
- **Important correctness detail found while reading the real codebase**: a trade's raw `t["strategy"]` field in `trades.json` is a fixed placeholder, not the real confirming strategy (`performance.py`'s own docstring on `primary_strategy_label`: *"the raw t['strategy'] field... is always the same hardcoded default"*) — the dashboard's own Strategy column already recomputes this per trade via `primary_strategy_label(t)` rather than trusting the stored field. The heatmap must do the same, or every trade silently groups into one wrong bucket.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_pages.py (append)

def test_strategy_heatmap_colors_and_na_cells(client, auth, monkeypatch):

        "entry": 100.0, "stop_loss": 95.0, "take_profit": 110.0, "exit_price": 110.0,
        "opened_at": "2026-01-01T00:00:00+00:00", "closed_at": "2026-01-02T00:00:00+00:00",
        "confidence_level": 3, "confidence_score": 60, "strategy": "RSI", "horizon_key": "4w",
    } for i in range(6)]  # 6 RSI/4w wins -> WR 100%, n=6
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_pages.py -k heatmap -v`
Expected: FAIL — no `.heatmap-grid` markup exists yet on `/strategies`.

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.analytics.aggregate import stats_by
from swingbot.core.backtest import ALL_STRATEGIES
from swingbot.core.performance import TradeLog, primary_strategy_label
from swingbot.core.strategy_types import HORIZONS


def _lerp_hex(c1: str, c2: str, t: float) -> str:
    r1, g1, b1 = int(c1[1:3], 16), int(c1[3:5], 16), int(c1[5:7], 16)
    r2, g2, b2 = int(c2[1:3], 16), int(c2[3:5], 16), int(c2[5:7], 16)
    r = round(r1 + (r2 - r1) * t)
    g = round(g1 + (g2 - g1) * t)
    b = round(b1 + (b2 - b1) * t)
    return f"#{r:02x}{g:02x}{b:02x}"


def _heatmap_color(win_rate: float) -> str:
    """Linear red (<=60) -> amber (75) -> green (>=85)."""
    if win_rate <= 60:
        return "#da6d6d"
    if win_rate >= 85:
        return "#6dda9e"
    if win_rate <= 75:
        return _lerp_hex("#da6d6d", "#e2b25a", (win_rate - 60) / 15)
    return _lerp_hex("#e2b25a", "#6dda9e", (win_rate - 75) / 10)


def _strategy_horizon_heatmap() -> dict:
    """Live win-rate per (strategy, horizon) cell. ASSUMED SHAPE:
    aggregate.stats_by(trades, keys=("strategy","horizon_key")) returns
    {(strategy, horizon): {"n": int, "win_rate": float | None}} -- confirm
    against Plan A's real implementation at merge. Relabels each trade's
    strategy via primary_strategy_label first (see this task's note above
    on why the raw t["strategy"] field can't be trusted)."""
    tl = TradeLog()
    closed = [t for t in tl.get_trades(status=None, limit=None) if t["status"] in ("win", "loss", "closed")]
    labeled = [{**t, "strategy": primary_strategy_label(t)} for t in closed]
    grouped = stats_by(labeled, keys=("strategy", "horizon_key"))
    horizons = list(HORIZONS.keys())
    matrix = {(s, h): grouped.get((s, h), {"n": 0, "win_rate": None}) for s in ALL_STRATEGIES for h in horizons}
    return {"strategies": list(ALL_STRATEGIES), "horizons": horizons, "matrix": matrix}
```

```diff
 @pages.route("/strategies", methods=["GET"])
 @require_auth
 def strategies_page():
-    return _render("Strategies", "strategies", "strategies.html", rows=_registry_rows())
+    return _render("Strategies", "strategies", "strategies.html",
+                   rows=_registry_rows(), heatmap=_strategy_horizon_heatmap(),
+                   heatmap_color=_heatmap_color)
```

```jinja
<div class="card">
  <p class="card-title">Strategy × horizon live win rate</p>
  <div style="overflow-x:auto;">
  <div class="heatmap-grid" style="grid-template-columns: 140px repeat({{ heatmap.horizons | length }}, 1fr); min-width:640px;">
    <div class="hm-header"></div>
    {% for h in heatmap.horizons %}<div class="hm-header">{{ h }}</div>{% endfor %}
    {% for s in heatmap.strategies %}
      <div class="hm-header" style="justify-content:flex-start;text-align:left;">{{ s }}</div>
      {% for h in heatmap.horizons %}
        {% set cell = heatmap.matrix[(s, h)] %}
        {% if cell.n < 5 %}
        <div class="hm-cell hm-na" title="{{ s }} / {{ h }}: n={{ cell.n }} (too few trades)">n/a</div>
        {% else %}
        <div class="hm-cell" style="background:{{ heatmap_color(cell.win_rate) }};"
             title="{{ s }} / {{ h }}: {{ '%.0f'|format(cell.win_rate) }}% (n={{ cell.n }})">
          {{ "%.0f"|format(cell.win_rate) }}% ({{ cell.n }})
        </div>
        {% endif %}
      {% endfor %}
    {% endfor %}
  </div>
  </div>
</div>
```

### Task C23: Rolling-WR sparklines

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/pages.py` (sparkline SVG helper), `swingbot/admin/templates/strategies.html`; test `tests/admin/test_pages.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `_sparkline_svg(points: list[float], *, width=120, height=28, ref: float | None = 80.0) -> str` (inline `<svg>` polyline, dashed reference line) in `pages.py` — reused verbatim by Task C43's dashboard equity card; a per-strategy sparkline of rolling win rate (window 10) over that strategy's own closed trades. Empty data → `&mdash;`.
- This is a **display-derived** computation, not a new analytics formula: a rolling win-rate over a trade sequence is the same category of "small per-row arithmetic helper" `app.py` already writes inline (`_closed_pnl`, `_closed_r`, `_format_duration_hms` are none of them analytics calls either — they're per-trade display math). It is written once here rather than duplicated per template.

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add near the heatmap helpers

def _rolling_win_rate_series(closed_trades: list[dict], window: int = 10) -> list[float | None]:
    """Rolling win-rate (0-100 scale) over a strategy's own closed-trade
    sequence, ordered by closed_at. Same "small per-trade display helper"
    category as app.py's _closed_pnl/_closed_r -- not an analytics call,
    just windowed arithmetic for a sparkline."""
    ordered = sorted(closed_trades, key=lambda t: t.get("closed_at") or "")
    outcomes = [1 if t["status"] == "win" else 0 for t in ordered if t["status"] in ("win", "loss")]
    points: list[float | None] = []
    for i in range(len(outcomes)):
        chunk = outcomes[max(0, i - window + 1):i + 1]
        points.append(sum(chunk) / len(chunk) * 100 if chunk else None)
    return points


def _sparkline_svg(points: list, *, width: int = 120, height: int = 28,
                    ref: float | None = 80.0) -> str:
    """Inline <svg> polyline sparkline over a 0-100 scale. `ref` draws a
    dashed horizontal reference line (the 80% OOS win-rate bar) so the eye
    has a fixed anchor point. Reused verbatim by Task C43's dashboard
    equity-curve card. Empty data -> em-dash (nothing to draw)."""
    pts = [p for p in points if p is not None]
    if not pts:
        return "&mdash;"
    n = len(pts)

    def _xy(i, v):
        x = (i / max(n - 1, 1)) * width
        y = height - (v / 100.0) * height
        return f"{x:.1f},{y:.1f}"

    poly = " ".join(_xy(i, v) for i, v in enumerate(pts))
    last = pts[-1]
    color = "#6dda9e" if last >= 80 else ("#e2b25a" if last >= 60 else "#da6d6d")
    ref_line = ""
    if ref is not None:
        ry = height - (ref / 100.0) * height
        ref_line = f'<polyline class="spark-ref" stroke="#9aa0b0" points="0,{ry:.1f} {width},{ry:.1f}" />'
    return (
        f'<svg class="sparkline" width="{width}" height="{height}" viewBox="0 0 {width} {height}">'
        f"{ref_line}"
        f'<polyline class="spark-line" stroke="{color}" points="{poly}" />'
        f"</svg>"
    )
```

```diff
 @pages.route("/strategies", methods=["GET"])
 @require_auth
 def strategies_page():
-    return _render("Strategies", "strategies", "strategies.html",
-                   rows=_registry_rows(), heatmap=_strategy_horizon_heatmap(),
-                   heatmap_color=_heatmap_color)
+    rows = _registry_rows()
+    tl = TradeLog()
+    closed = [t for t in tl.get_trades(status=None, limit=None) if t["status"] in ("win", "loss", "closed")]
+    labeled = [{**t, "strategy": primary_strategy_label(t)} for t in closed]
+    for row in rows:
+        strat_trades = [t for t in labeled if t["strategy"] == row["strategy"]]
+        row["sparkline_svg"] = _sparkline_svg(_rolling_win_rate_series(strat_trades, window=10))
+    return _render("Strategies", "strategies", "strategies.html",
+                   rows=rows, heatmap=_strategy_horizon_heatmap(), heatmap_color=_heatmap_color)
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
import json
```

```python
@pages.route("/calibration", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def calibration_page():
    snap = load_snapshot(max_age_seconds=3600) or refresh_snapshot()
    calibration = (snap or {}).get("calibration", {})
    chart_data_json = json.dumps({"deciles": calibration.get("deciles", [])})
    return _render(
        "Calibration", "calibration", "calibration.html",
        tiers=calibration.get("tiers", []), drift=calibration.get("drift", []),
        chart_data_json=chart_data_json,
    )
```

```jinja
{# swingbot/admin/templates/calibration.html -- full replacement #}
{% extends "base.html" %}
{% block body %}
<script id="chart-data" type="application/json">{{ chart_data_json | safe }}</script>

<div class="card">
  <p class="card-title">What is calibration?</p>
  <p class="muted" style="font-size:13px;line-height:1.6;margin:0;">
    Calibration asks one question: does a higher confidence score actually win more? Every closed
    trade is bucketed into a decile by its confidence score at entry, and each decile's realized win
    rate is plotted against the 80% target line below. A well-calibrated system produces a roughly
    upward-sloping staircase — top-decile trades should win noticeably more often than bottom-decile
    trades. A flat or inverted staircase means the score isn't actually predictive yet and needs
    revisiting before it's trusted for sizing or filtering decisions.
  </p>
</div>

<div class="chart-card">
  <div class="chart-title">📐 Score deciles — realized win rate vs 80% target</div>
  <div class="chart-wrap" style="height:220px;">
    <canvas id="chart-deciles"></canvas>
  </div>
</div>

<div class="card">
  <p class="card-title">Tier calibration</p>
  <div style="overflow-x:auto;">
  <table>
    <thead><tr><th>Tier</th><th>N</th><th>Live WR</th><th>Expected band</th><th>Pass</th></tr></thead>
    <tbody>
    {% for row in tiers %}
    <tr>
      <td><span class="chip chip-tier-{{ row.tier | lower }}">{{ row.tier }}</span></td>
      <td>{{ row.n }}</td>
      <td>{{ "%.1f%%"|format(row.win_rate) if row.win_rate is not none else '—' }}</td>
      <td class="muted">{{ row.expected_band }}</td>
      <td>{% if row.pass %}✅{% elif row.pass is sameas false %}❌{% else %}—{% endif %}</td>
    </tr>
    {% endfor %}
    </tbody>
  </table>
  </div>
</div>

<div class="card">
  <p class="card-title">Badge drift</p>
  <div style="overflow-x:auto;">
  <table>
    <thead><tr><th>Strategy</th><th>Live WR</th><th>OOS WR</th><th>Δ</th><th>Decayed</th></tr></thead>
    <tbody>
    {% for d in drift %}
    <tr>
      <td>{{ d.strategy }}</td>
      <td>{{ "%.1f%%"|format(d.live_wr) if d.live_wr is not none else '—' }}</td>
      <td>{{ "%.1f%%"|format(d.oos_wr) if d.oos_wr is not none else '—' }}</td>
      <td style="color:{% if d.delta is none %}#5a6275{% elif d.delta < 0 %}#da6d6d{% else %}#6dda9e{% endif %};">
        {{ "%+.1f"|format(d.delta) if d.delta is not none else '—' }}
      </td>
      <td>{% if d.decayed %}<span class="chip chip-decay">DECAY</span>{% else %}—{% endif %}</td>
    </tr>
    {% endfor %}
    </tbody>
  </table>
  </div>
</div>

<script>
(function () {
  "use strict";
  var raw = JSON.parse(document.getElementById('chart-data').textContent);
  var deciles = raw.deciles || [];
  new Chart(document.getElementById('chart-deciles'), {
    type: 'bar',
    data: {
      labels: deciles.map(function (d) { return 'D' + d.decile; }),
      datasets: [{
        label: 'Realized win rate %',
        data: deciles.map(function (d) { return d.win_rate; }),
        backgroundColor: deciles.map(function (d) { return d.win_rate >= 80 ? 'rgba(109,218,158,.75)' : 'rgba(226,178,90,.75)'; }),
      }],
    },
    options: {
      responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
      plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
      scales: {
        y: { min: 0, max: 100, grid: { color: '#1a1d26' }, ticks: { color: '#5a6275' } },
        x: { grid: { color: '#1a1d26' }, ticks: { color: '#5a6275' } },
      },
    },
    plugins: [{
      id: 'target-line',
      afterDraw: function (chart) {
        var yScale = chart.scales.y;
        var ctx = chart.ctx;
        var y = yScale.getPixelForValue(80);
        ctx.save();
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#6ea8fe';
        ctx.setLineDash([4, 4]);
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(chart.chartArea.left, y);
        ctx.lineTo(chart.chartArea.right, y);
        ctx.stroke();
        ctx.restore();
      },
    }],
  });
})();
</script>
{% endblock %}
```

```python
# tests/admin/test_pages.py (append)

class _FakeJournalStoreForPages:
    _ENTRIES = [
        {"trade_id": "t1", "ticker": "AAPL", "strategy": "RSI", "tags": ["clean_breakout"], "outcome": "win",
         "r_realized": 1.4, "mfe_r": 1.6, "mae_r": -0.2, "exit_efficiency": 0.87,
         "auto_lesson": "Waited for full confirmation before entering -- textbook execution.", "note": None},
        {"trade_id": "t2", "ticker": "MSFT", "strategy": "MACD", "tags": ["chased"], "outcome": "loss",
         "r_realized": -1.0, "mfe_r": 0.1, "mae_r": -1.0, "exit_efficiency": 0.0,
         "auto_lesson": "Entered after the move was already extended.", "note": "entered late"},
    ]

    def entries(self, strategy=None, tag=None, outcome=None, has_note=None, limit=200):
        rows = list(self._ENTRIES)
        if strategy:
            rows = [r for r in rows if r["strategy"] == strategy]
        if tag:
            rows = [r for r in rows if tag in r["tags"]]
        if outcome:
            rows = [r for r in rows if r["outcome"] == outcome]
        if has_note is not None:
            rows = [r for r in rows if (r["note"] is not None) == has_note]
        return rows[:limit]


def test_journal_page_filters_and_shows_lesson(client, auth, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.pages.JournalStore", _FakeJournalStoreForPages)
    r = client.get("/journal?tag=clean_breakout", headers=auth)
    html = r.data.decode("utf-8")
    assert "AAPL" in html
    assert "MSFT" not in html
    assert "textbook execution" in html
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.analytics.journal import JournalStore


def _parse_bool_param(v: str | None) -> bool | None:
    """Duplicated (deliberately) from api.py's identical 3-line helper --
    two independent blueprints, not worth a shared micro-module for this."""
    if v is None or v == "":
        return None
    return v.lower() in ("1", "true", "yes")


@pages.route("/journal", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def journal_page():
    strategy = request.args.get("strategy") or None
    tag = request.args.get("tag") or None
    outcome = request.args.get("outcome") or None
    has_note = _parse_bool_param(request.args.get("has_note"))
    store = JournalStore()
    entries = store.entries(strategy=strategy, tag=tag, outcome=outcome, has_note=has_note,
                            limit=int(request.args.get("limit", 200)))
    all_tags = sorted({t for e in store.entries(limit=10000) for t in (e.get("tags") or [])})
    filters = {
        "strategy": strategy or "", "tag": tag or "", "outcome": outcome or "",
        "has_note": request.args.get("has_note", ""),
    }
    return _render("Journal", "journal", "journal.html", view="entries",
                   entries=entries, all_tags=all_tags, filters=filters)
```

```diff
+document.querySelectorAll('.journal-note-form').forEach(function (form) {
+  form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
+    var tradeId = form.dataset.tradeId;
+    var textarea = form.querySelector('textarea[name="note"]');
+    var status = form.querySelector('.note-save-status');
+    status.textContent = 'Saving…';
+    fetch('/api/journal/' + encodeURIComponent(tradeId) + '/note', {
+      method: 'POST',
+      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },
+      body: 'note=' + encodeURIComponent(textarea.value),
+      credentials: 'include',
+    })
+      .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
+      .then(function (body) {
+        status.textContent = body.ok ? 'Saved ✓' : 'Not found';
+        setTimeout(function () { status.textContent = ''; }, 2000);
+      })
+      .catch(function () { status.textContent = 'Failed'; });
+  });
+});
+</script>
 {% endblock %}
```

# Phase C5 — Tuning workbench (Tasks C29–C37)

### Task C29: JobManager

**Files:**
- Create: `swingbot/admin/jobs.py`
- Modify: `tests/admin/conftest.py` (`_RELOAD_MODULES` gains `"swingbot.admin.jobs"`)
- Test: `tests/admin/test_jobs.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `class JobManager` (module instance `manager`): `start(kind: str, args: list[str]) -> str` (job_id; raises `RuntimeError("job already running")` if one is active — tuning is serialized), `status(job_id) -> dict | None`, `tail(job_id, n=100) -> str`, `all() -> list[dict]`. Runs `subprocess.Popen([sys.executable, script, *args], stdout=logfile, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)` in a daemon thread; state persisted to `data/admin_jobs.json` (survives an admin-process restart; a job found "running" at startup with a dead pid is reaped to `"failed"`). Log files under `logs/jobs/<job_id>.log`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_jobs.py
"""JobManager: subprocess job lifecycle. `kind="test"` allows a raw argv
(interpreter-relative) for tests -- `kind="tune"` (C31) always routes
through scripts/tune_strategy.py and the TRAIN-only guardrail."""
import time

import pytest


def _wait_until_done(mgr, job_id, timeout=5.0):
    deadline = time.time() + timeout
    while time.time() < deadline:
        status = mgr.status(job_id)
        if status and status["state"] in ("done", "failed"):
            return status
        time.sleep(0.05)
    raise TimeoutError(f"job {job_id} did not finish within {timeout}s")


def test_job_runs_and_tail_captures_output(admin_app):
    from swingbot.admin.jobs import JobManager
    mgr = JobManager()
    job_id = mgr.start("test", ["-c", "print('hi')"])
    status = _wait_until_done(mgr, job_id)
    assert status["state"] == "done"
    assert status["returncode"] == 0
    assert "hi" in mgr.tail(job_id)


def test_concurrent_start_raises_while_busy(admin_app):
    from swingbot.admin.jobs import JobManager
    mgr = JobManager()
    mgr.start("test", ["-c", "import time; time.sleep(2)"])
    with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match="already running"):
        mgr.start("test", ["-c", "print('should not start')"])
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_jobs.py -v`
Expected: FAIL — `ModuleNotFoundError: No module named 'swingbot.admin.jobs'`.

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/jobs.py
"""Subprocess job runner for admin-launched long-running work (currently:
TRAIN-window strategy tuning grids via scripts/tune_strategy.py). At most
ONE job runs at a time -- tuning is deliberately serialized, both because
concurrent grid sweeps would contend for the same OHLCV cache/CPU and
because the workbench UI (Task C33+) only has room to show one running
job's progress. State persisted to data/admin_jobs.json so a restart of
the admin process doesn't lose job history; a job found "running" at
startup whose pid is actually dead (the admin process or the subprocess
itself died mid-job -- e.g. a container restart) is reaped to "failed"
rather than permanently blocking every future job start.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
import re
import subprocess
import sys
import threading
import uuid
from datetime import datetime, timezone

from swingbot import config


def _jobs_path() -> str:
    return os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, "admin_jobs.json")


def _log_dir() -> str:
    d = os.path.join(config._PROJECT_ROOT, "logs", "jobs")
    os.makedirs(d, exist_ok=True)
    return d


def _read_jobs() -> dict:
    path = _jobs_path()
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return {}
    try:
        with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            return json.load(f)
    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
        return {}


def _write_jobs(jobs: dict) -> None:
    path = _jobs_path()
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(jobs, f, indent=2)


def _pid_alive(pid: int) -> bool:
    try:
        os.kill(pid, 0)
    except OSError:
        return False
    return True


class JobManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self._lock = threading.Lock()

    def _any_active(self, jobs: dict) -> bool:
        for job in jobs.values():
            if job["state"] in ("queued", "running"):
                if job.get("pid") and not _pid_alive(job["pid"]):
                    continue  # stale -- _reap_stale will mark it failed
                return True
        return False

    def _reap_stale(self, jobs: dict) -> None:
        changed = False
        for job in jobs.values():
            if job["state"] in ("queued", "running") and job.get("pid") and not _pid_alive(job["pid"]):
                job["state"] = "failed"
                job["finished_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
                job["returncode"] = None
                changed = True
        if changed:
            _write_jobs(jobs)

    def start(self, kind: str, args: list[str]) -> str:
        with self._lock:
            jobs = _read_jobs()
            self._reap_stale(jobs)
            if self._any_active(jobs):
                raise RuntimeError("job already running")

            job_id = uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]
            log_path = os.path.join(_log_dir(), f"{job_id}.log")
            if kind == "tune":
                script = os.path.join(config._PROJECT_ROOT, "scripts", "tune_strategy.py")
                argv = [sys.executable, script, *args]
            else:
                # kind="test" (or any other future raw-argv kind) -- args is
                # the full argv tail after the interpreter itself.
                argv = [sys.executable, *args]

            logfile = open(log_path, "w", encoding="utf-8")
            proc = subprocess.Popen(argv, stdout=logfile, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)

            jobs[job_id] = {
                "id": job_id, "kind": kind, "args": args, "state": "running",
                "started_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(), "finished_at": None,
                "returncode": None, "log_path": log_path, "pid": proc.pid,
            }
            _write_jobs(jobs)

            def _watch():
                proc.wait()
                logfile.close()
                with self._lock:
                    j = _read_jobs()
                    if job_id in j:
                        j[job_id]["state"] = "done" if proc.returncode == 0 else "failed"
                        j[job_id]["finished_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
                        j[job_id]["returncode"] = proc.returncode
                        _write_jobs(j)

            threading.Thread(target=_watch, daemon=True).start()
            return job_id

    def status(self, job_id: str) -> dict | None:
        jobs = _read_jobs()
        self._reap_stale(jobs)
        return _read_jobs().get(job_id)

    def tail(self, job_id: str, n: int = 100) -> str:
        job = self.status(job_id)
        if not job or not os.path.exists(job["log_path"]):
            return ""
        with open(job["log_path"], "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="replace") as f:
            lines = f.readlines()
        return "".join(lines[-n:])

    def all(self) -> list[dict]:
        jobs = _read_jobs()
        self._reap_stale(jobs)
        return sorted(_read_jobs().values(), key=lambda j: j["started_at"], reverse=True)


manager = JobManager()
```

### Task C30: Job API

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/api.py`; test `tests/admin/test_jobs.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `POST /api/jobs/tune` (form: `strategy`, optional `params` — a JSON-encoded dict, whitelisted starting Task C31) → `{"job_id": ...}`, or **409** `{"error": "busy"}` when a job is already active; `GET /api/jobs/<id>` → the status dict + `log_tail` (last 50 log lines); `GET /api/jobs` → the most recent 20.
- This task's `/api/jobs/tune` builds its argv directly (`["--strategy", strategy]`) as a placeholder — Task C31 replaces that line with `build_tune_args(strategy, params)`, the guardrail's only legal entry point.

```python
# swingbot/admin/api.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.admin.jobs import manager as job_manager


@api.route("/jobs/tune", methods=["POST"])
@require_auth_json
def api_jobs_tune():
    strategy = request.form.get("strategy", "")
    args = ["--strategy", strategy]  # Task C31 replaces this line with build_tune_args(strategy, params)
    try:
        job_id = job_manager.start("tune", args)
    except RuntimeError:
        return jsonify({"error": "busy"}), 409
    return jsonify({"job_id": job_id})


@api.route("/jobs/<job_id>", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth_json
def api_job_status(job_id):
    status = job_manager.status(job_id)
    if not status:
        return jsonify({"error": "not found"}), 404
    return jsonify({**status, "log_tail": job_manager.tail(job_id, n=50)})


@api.route("/jobs", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth_json
def api_jobs_list():
    return jsonify({"jobs": job_manager.all()[:20]})
```

### Task C31: TRAIN-only guardrail

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/jobs.py`, `swingbot/admin/api.py` (wire `build_tune_args` into `/api/jobs/tune`); test `tests/admin/test_jobs.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `build_tune_args(strategy: str, params: dict | None) -> list[str]` — the ONLY constructor of tuning argv: whitelists `strategy` against `backtest.ALL_STRATEGIES`, always appends the fixed TRAIN flags `scripts/tune_strategy.py` actually accepts today (`--strategy`, optional `--be-trigger`), accepts no date argument at all. `assert_train_only(args)` raises `ValueError` on any `--from`/`--to`/`--validation` token or any bare date string `>= 2024-01-01`; `JobManager.start(kind="tune", ...)` calls it unconditionally (defense-in-depth even if a caller somehow bypasses `build_tune_args`). Module constants `VALIDATION_WINDOW = ("2024-01-01", "2025-12-31")` and `TRAIN_WINDOW = ("2020-01-01", "2023-12-31")` (the exact window `tune_strategy.py` itself hard-codes as `TRAIN`, per this plan's ground-truth deviation #3), both with docstrings explaining WHY.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_jobs.py (append)

def test_guardrail_blocks_validation_window():
    from swingbot.admin.jobs import assert_train_only, build_tune_args
    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
        assert_train_only(["--from", "2024-06-01", "--to", "2024-12-31"])
    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
        assert_train_only(["--validation"])
    assert_train_only(build_tune_args("RSI", None))  # must not raise

    from swingbot.admin.jobs import build_tune_args
    with pytest.raises(ValueError, match="unknown strategy"):
        build_tune_args("Not A Real Strategy", None)

    from swingbot.admin.jobs import build_tune_args
    args = build_tune_args("RSI", {"be_trigger": 0.6})
    assert args == ["--strategy", "RSI", "--be-trigger", "0.6"]

    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
```

Expected: FAIL — `ImportError: cannot import name 'assert_train_only'`.

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/jobs.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.core.backtest import ALL_STRATEGIES

# The out-of-sample window already consumed by round-1 validation
# (docs/superpowers/results/2026-07-validation.md). Reusing it for
# parameter SELECTION is silent overfitting: any "improvement" measured
# against a window whose numbers already informed strategy/gate choices
# is no longer really out-of-sample. Tuning stays on TRAIN below;
# VALIDATION is run once, manually, via the CLI (scripts/run_backtest_range.py
# --validation), never through this admin UI.
VALIDATION_WINDOW = ("2024-01-01", "2025-12-31")

# What scripts/tune_strategy.py itself hard-codes as TRAIN today (see this
# plan's ground-truth deviation #3 -- the script has no date CLI flag at
# all yet; this constant is shown on the Tuning page so the window is
# visible even though it can't be changed from here).
TRAIN_WINDOW = ("2020-01-01", "2023-12-31")

_DATE_LIKE = re.compile(r"^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$")
_BANNED_DATE_FLAGS = {"--from", "--to", "--validation"}


def assert_train_only(args: list[str]) -> None:
    """The ONLY gate standing between the admin UI and scripts/tune_strategy.py
    ever being pointed at the VALIDATION window. Today's tune_strategy.py CLI
    doesn't even accept a date flag (ground-truth deviation #3) -- this is
    defense-in-depth against a FUTURE version of the script gaining one, not
    a fix for a live vulnerability. Raises ValueError on any --from/--to/
    --validation token, or any bare YYYY-MM-DD date string >= 2024-01-01."""
    for tok in args:
        if tok in _BANNED_DATE_FLAGS:
            raise ValueError(f"tuning args may not include {tok!r} (VALIDATION window is off-limits)")
        if _DATE_LIKE.match(tok) and tok >= VALIDATION_WINDOW[0]:
            raise ValueError(f"tuning args may not reference a date >= {VALIDATION_WINDOW[0]} ({tok!r})")


def build_tune_args(strategy: str, params: dict | None) -> list[str]:
    """THE only constructor of a tuning job's argv. Whitelists strategy
    against backtest.ALL_STRATEGIES, appends only the flags
    scripts/tune_strategy.py actually accepts today (--strategy,
    optional --be-trigger), and accepts no date argument at all. Every
    call site (api.py's /api/jobs/tune) must route through this."""
    if strategy not in ALL_STRATEGIES:
        raise ValueError(f"unknown strategy {strategy!r}; must be one of {ALL_STRATEGIES}")
    args = ["--strategy", strategy]
    if params and "be_trigger" in params:
        args += ["--be-trigger", str(float(params["be_trigger"]))]
    assert_train_only(args)
    return args
```

```diff
 class JobManager:
     def start(self, kind: str, args: list[str]) -> str:
+        if kind == "tune":
+            assert_train_only(args)
         with self._lock:
             jobs = _read_jobs()
```

```diff
     strategy = request.form.get("strategy", "")
-    args = ["--strategy", strategy]  # Task C31 replaces this line with build_tune_args(strategy, params)
+    params_raw = request.form.get("params")
+    params = json.loads(params_raw) if params_raw else None
+    try:
+        args = build_tune_args(strategy, params)
+    except ValueError as e:
+        return jsonify({"error": str(e)}), 400
     try:
         job_id = job_manager.start("tune", args)
     except RuntimeError:
         return jsonify({"error": "busy"}), 409
     return jsonify({"job_id": job_id})
```
