```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.core import entry_filters
from swingbot.core.registry import get_badge


@pages.route("/tuning", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def tuning_page():
    strategy_filter = request.args.get("strategy") or None
    strategies = [strategy_filter] if strategy_filter else list(ALL_STRATEGIES)
    current_state = []
    for s in strategies:
        badge = get_badge("strategy", s)
        current_state.append({
            "strategy": s,
            "gate_description": _gate_description(s),
            "rr_override": STRATEGY_RR_OVERRIDE.get(s),
            "default_params": dict(entry_filters.DEFAULT_PARAMS.get(s, {})),
            "badge": badge.status, "window": badge.window, "run_date": badge.run_date,
        })
    return _render("Tuning", "tuning", "tuning.html", current_state=current_state,
                   strategy_filter=strategy_filter or "")
```

Replace the C5 shell `tuning_page()` with this one (same function name, same route).

```jinja
  </p>
  <div style="overflow-x:auto;">
  <table>
    <thead>
      <tr><th>Strategy</th><th>Badge</th><th>R:R</th><th>Gate</th><th>Default params</th><th>Window</th><th>Run date</th></tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody>
    {% for s in current_state %}
    <tr>
      <td><strong>{{ s.strategy }}</strong></td>
      <td><span class="chip {{ 'chip-validated' if s.badge == 'VALIDATED' else 'chip-weak' }}">{{ s.badge }}</span></td>
      <td>{{ "%.2f"|format(s.rr_override) if s.rr_override is not none else '—' }}</td>
      <td class="muted">{{ s.gate_description }}</td>
      <td class="muted">
        {% for k, v in s.default_params.items() %}{{ k }}={{ v }}{% if not loop.last %}, {% endif %}{% endfor %}
      </td>
      <td class="muted">{{ s.window }}</td>
      <td class="muted">{{ s.run_date }}</td>
    </tr>
    {% endfor %}
    </tbody>
  </table>
  </div>
```

```jinja
{# swingbot/admin/templates/tuning.html -- append after the "Current
   parameters" card #}
<div class="card">
  <p class="card-title">Run TRAIN grid</p>
  {% if running_job %}
  <div class="empty-state" style="padding:20px;">
    <p>A tuning job is already running (<code>{{ running_job.id }}</code>) — see progress below.
       Only one tuning job runs at a time.</p>
  </div>
  {% else %}
  <div class="banner" style="border-left:3px solid #6ea8fe;margin-bottom:12px;">
    TRAIN window (fixed, immutable): {{ train_window[0] }} .. {{ train_window[1] }} — no date input
    is exposed on this page or anywhere in this workbench.
  </div>
  <form id="tune-launch-form" onsubmit="return false;">
    <div style="margin-bottom:10px;">
      <label class="muted" style="font-size:12px;display:block;margin-bottom:4px;">Strategy</label>
      <select name="strategy" id="tune-strategy-select"
              style="background:#13161d;color:#dde1ea;border:1px solid #1f2330;border-radius:6px;padding:6px 10px;font-size:13px;">
        {% for s in all_strategies %}
        <option value="{{ s }}" {{ 'selected' if s == strategy_filter else '' }}>{{ s }}</option>
        {% endfor %}
      </select>
    </div>
    <button type="submit" class="small">▶ Launch TRAIN grid</button>
    <span class="muted" id="tune-launch-status" style="font-size:12px;margin-left:8px;"></span>
  </form>
  <script>
  document.getElementById('tune-launch-form').addEventListener('submit', function () {
    var strategy = document.getElementById('tune-strategy-select').value;
    var status = document.getElementById('tune-launch-status');
    status.textContent = 'Launching…';
    fetch('/api/jobs/tune', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },
      body: 'strategy=' + encodeURIComponent(strategy),
      credentials: 'include',
    })
      .then(function (r) { return r.json().then(function (body) { return { httpStatus: r.status, body: body }; }); })
      .then(function (res) {
        if (res.httpStatus === 409) { status.textContent = 'Busy — a job is already running.'; return; }
        if (res.httpStatus !== 200) { status.textContent = 'Error: ' + (res.body.error || 'unknown'); return; }
        window.location.reload();  // now running -- reload shows the progress card (Task C34)
      })
      .catch(function () { status.textContent = 'Request failed.'; });
  });
  </script>
  {% endif %}
</div>
```

- [ ] **Step 3: PASS, Step 4: Commit**

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_pages.py -k grid_launch -v` → 2 passed.

```bash
git commit -m "feat: grid launch form"
```

### Task C35: Results comparison

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/pages.py`, `swingbot/admin/templates/tuning.html`, `scripts/tune_strategy.py` (add `--json PATH` output — confirmed missing per this plan's ground-truth deviation #3)
- Test: `tests/admin/test_jobs.py`, `tests/scripts/test_tune_strategy.py` (new — the script's own mini-test for the new flag)

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `JobManager.start(kind="tune", ...)` now also appends `--json <data/tuning_results/<job_id>.json>` to the argv itself (out-of-band from `build_tune_args`'s whitelisted args — the job's own id, hence its own result path, doesn't exist until `start()` generates it), and records that path on the job dict as `"result_path"`. `scripts/tune_strategy.py --json PATH` writes `{strategy, grid: [{params, n_eval, win_rate, expectancy_r, excluded_share}], best: {...} | None}`. `/tuning?job_id=<id>` renders a finished job's grid as a table, current in-code params implicitly visible via the "Current parameters" card above, and pass-gate rows (`N>=30, WR>=80, ExpR>0, excl<=50%`) tinted via the existing `.diff-add` class. `_load_result(job_id) -> dict | None` and `_grid_row_passes(stats) -> bool` in `pages.py`.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test — the script's own `--json` flag**

```python
import json

def test_tune_strategy_writes_json_output(tmp_path, monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr(ts, "load_watchlist", lambda: ["AAA"])
    monkeypatch.setattr(ts, "load_cached", lambda ticker: object())  # never read -- run_config is stubbed below
    monkeypatch.setattr(ts, "run_config", lambda strategy, dfs: {
        "n_eval": 40, "win_rate": 82.0, "expectancy_r": 0.09, "excluded_share": 0.2,
    })
    out_path = tmp_path / "result.json"
    monkeypatch.setattr(sys, "argv", ["tune_strategy.py", "--strategy", "MACD", "--json", str(out_path)])
    ts.main()
    payload = json.loads(out_path.read_text())
    assert payload["strategy"] == "MACD"
    assert len(payload["grid"]) == 3  # MACD's PARAM_GRID has one key ("ext_atr"), 3 values
    assert payload["best"]["win_rate"] == 82.0
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from swingbot.core.strategy_types import HORIZONS  # already imported (C21) -- kept for clarity


def _load_result(job_id: str) -> dict | None:
    path = os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, "tuning_results", f"{job_id}.json")
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return None
    try:
        with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            return json.load(f)
    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
        return None


def _grid_row_passes(stats: dict) -> bool:
    """Same acceptance gate scripts/tune_strategy.py itself already prints
    ("N/A configs qualify (WR>=80, ExpR>0, N>=30, excl<=50%)") -- restated
    here purely to color a table row, never to decide anything."""
    return (
        stats.get("n_eval", 0) >= 30 and (stats.get("win_rate") or 0) >= 80
        and (stats.get("expectancy_r") or 0) > 0 and stats.get("excluded_share", 1) <= 0.5
    )
```

```diff
 @pages.route("/tuning", methods=["GET"])
 @require_auth
 def tuning_page():
     ...
     recent_jobs = job_manager.all()[:5]
+    job_id_param = request.args.get("job_id")
+    result = _load_result(job_id_param) if job_id_param else None
     return _render("Tuning", "tuning", "tuning.html", current_state=current_state,
                    strategy_filter=strategy_filter or "", running_job=running_job,
                    all_strategies=list(ALL_STRATEGIES), train_window=TRAIN_WINDOW,
-                   recent_jobs=recent_jobs)
+                   recent_jobs=recent_jobs, result=result, job_id_param=job_id_param,
+                   grid_row_passes=_grid_row_passes)
```

Add `import json`, `import os` to `pages.py`'s imports if not already present from earlier tasks (C25 added `json`; `os` is new here).

```jinja
<div class="card">
  <p class="card-title">Results — {{ result.strategy }} (job {{ job_id_param }})</p>
  <div style="overflow-x:auto;">
  <table>
    <thead>
      <tr><th>Params</th><th>N</th><th>Win rate</th><th>ExpR</th><th>Excl%</th><th>Pass</th></tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody>
    {% for row in result.grid %}
    <tr class="{{ 'diff-add' if grid_row_passes(row) else '' }}">
      <td class="muted">
        {% for k, v in row.params.items() %}{{ k }}={{ v }}{% if not loop.last %}, {% endif %}{% endfor %}
      </td>
      <td>{{ row.n_eval }}</td>
      <td>{{ "%.1f%%"|format(row.win_rate) if row.win_rate is not none else '—' }}</td>
      <td>{{ "%+.3f"|format(row.expectancy_r) if row.expectancy_r is not none else '—' }}</td>
      <td>{{ "%.0f%%"|format(row.excluded_share * 100) }}</td>
      <td>{% if grid_row_passes(row) %}✅{% else %}—{% endif %}</td>
    </tr>
    {% endfor %}
    </tbody>
  </table>
  </div>
</div>
```

```python
def test_tuning_propose_writes_file_with_all_keys(client, auth):
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py -- add to imports
from datetime import datetime, timezone

TUNING_PROPOSALS_DIR_NAME = "tuning_proposals"


@pages.route("/tuning/propose", methods=["POST"])
@require_auth
def tuning_propose():
    job_id = request.form.get("job_id", "")
    try:
        row_index = int(request.form.get("row_index", "-1"))
    except ValueError:
        abort(400, "Invalid row index.")
    result = _load_result(job_id)
    if not result or row_index < 0 or row_index >= len(result.get("grid", [])):
        abort(404, "Could not find that job/row.")

    row = result["grid"][row_index]
    strategy = result["strategy"]
    proposal = {
        "strategy": strategy,
        "proposed_params": row["params"],
        "train_stats": {k: v for k, v in row.items() if k != "params"},
        "current_params": dict(entry_filters.DEFAULT_PARAMS.get(strategy, {})),
        "job_id": job_id,
        "created_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        "note": (
            "Apply by editing entry_filters.DEFAULT_PARAMS, run the suite, and only then "
            "consider a validation shot — remembering the window is spent."
        ),
    }
    proposals_dir = os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, TUNING_PROPOSALS_DIR_NAME)
    os.makedirs(proposals_dir, exist_ok=True)
    ts_slug = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y%m%d%H%M%S")
    strat_slug = strategy.lower().replace(" ", "-").replace("/", "-").replace("&", "and")
    fname = f"{ts_slug}-{strat_slug}.json"
    with open(os.path.join(proposals_dir, fname), "w") as f:
        json.dump(proposal, f, indent=2)
    return redirect(url_for("pages.tuning_page", job_id=job_id, msg=f"Proposal saved: {fname}", ok=1))
```

```diff
 {# swingbot/admin/templates/tuning.html -- C35's results table gains an
    Action column #}
-      <tr><th>Params</th><th>N</th><th>Win rate</th><th>ExpR</th><th>Excl%</th><th>Pass</th></tr>
+      <tr><th>Params</th><th>N</th><th>Win rate</th><th>ExpR</th><th>Excl%</th><th>Pass</th><th>Action</th></tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
     {% for row in result.grid %}
     <tr class="{{ 'diff-add' if grid_row_passes(row) else '' }}">
       ...
       <td>{% if grid_row_passes(row) %}✅{% else %}—{% endif %}</td>
+      <td>
+        <form method="post" action="{{ url_for('pages.tuning_propose') }}" style="margin:0;">
+          <input type="hidden" name="job_id" value="{{ job_id_param }}">
+          <input type="hidden" name="row_index" value="{{ loop.index0 }}">
+          <button type="submit" class="secondary small">Propose</button>
+        </form>
+      </td>
     </tr>
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/pages.py

def _list_proposals() -> list[dict]:
    proposals_dir = os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, TUNING_PROPOSALS_DIR_NAME)
    if not os.path.exists(proposals_dir):
        return []
    rows = []
    for fname in sorted(os.listdir(proposals_dir), reverse=True):
        if not fname.endswith(".json"):
            continue
        try:
            with open(os.path.join(proposals_dir, fname), "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            rows.append({"filename": fname, **data})
        except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
            continue
    return rows


@pages.route("/tuning/proposals/<filename>/delete", methods=["POST"])
@require_auth
def tuning_proposal_delete(filename):
    proposals_dir = os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, TUNING_PROPOSALS_DIR_NAME)
    path = os.path.join(proposals_dir, filename)
    if filename.endswith(".json") and os.path.exists(path):
        os.remove(path)
    return redirect(url_for("pages.tuning_page", msg=f"Deleted proposal {filename}.", ok=1))
```

# Phase C6 — Settings v2 (Tasks C38–C41)

### Task C38: Diff preview before save

**Files:**
- Modify: `swingbot/admin/helpers.py` (new `settings_diff(form, existing) -> list[dict]`), `swingbot/admin/app.py` (new `POST /settings/preview`, importing `settings_diff` into the existing `from .helpers import (...)` block at lines 66–72), `swingbot/admin/templates/settings.html` (modal + intercepted submit, inserted right after the form's closing `</form>` at line 97 and inside the `.save-bar` div at lines 93–96)
- Test: `tests/admin/test_settings_v2.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `settings_diff(form, existing) -> list[dict]` returns `[{key, label, old, new, sensitive}]` for changed fields only, sensitive values masked `"•••"` on **both** sides (never shown even briefly in a diff preview); `POST /settings/preview` renders a small HTML fragment (`_settings_diff.html`) with the diff table, or "Nothing changed." when the diff is empty. The Save button's `submit` handler is intercepted client-side: it first `fetch()`es the preview into a confirm modal; only the modal's own "Confirm & Save" button does the real form submit to the existing, unchanged `/settings/save` endpoint.

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement `settings_diff` in `helpers.py`**

```python
# swingbot/admin/helpers.py -- add near _changed_non_hot_reloadable_fields

def settings_diff(form, existing: dict) -> list[dict]:
    """[{key, label, old, new, sensitive}] for CHANGED fields only --
    sensitive values masked "•••" on both sides regardless of what they
    actually changed to/from, since this is rendered straight into an
    HTML fragment the browser (and, via /settings/preview, the network)
    sees. Mirrors _build_env_text's own "blank form value == no change"
    rule so the diff and the actual save never disagree about what
    counts as a real change."""
    changed = []
    for f in config.FIELDS:
        old = existing.get(f.key, f.default)
        if f.type == "checkbox":
            new = "true" if form.get(f.key) == "on" else "false"
        else:
            new = form.get(f.key, old)
            if new == "" and f.key in existing:
                new = old
        if str(old) == str(new):
            continue
        display_old = "•••" if f.sensitive else old
        display_new = "•••" if f.sensitive else new
        changed.append({"key": f.key, "label": f.label, "old": display_old,
                        "new": display_new, "sensitive": f.sensitive})
    return changed
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/helpers.py -- add near settings_diff
AUDIT_LOG_PATH = os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, "settings_audit.jsonl")


def _audit_log_path() -> str:
    # Resolved at call time (not module-import time) so tests that
    # monkeypatch config.DATA_DIR per-test are honored -- same reasoning
    # as PlanStore._path() and JobManager's _jobs_path().
    return os.path.join(config.DATA_DIR, "settings_audit.jsonl")


def append_settings_audit(diff: list) -> None:
    if not diff:
        return
    entry = {
        "ts": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        "changes": [{"key": d["key"], "old": d["old"], "new": d["new"]} for d in diff],
    }
    path = _audit_log_path()
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(json.dumps(entry) + "\n")


def read_settings_audit(n: int = 20) -> list[dict]:
    path = _audit_log_path()
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return []
    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        lines = f.readlines()
    rows = []
    for line in lines[-n:]:
        try:
            rows.append(json.loads(line))
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            continue
    return list(reversed(rows))
```

### Task C40: Export / import profiles

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/app.py` (`GET /settings/export`, `POST /settings/import`), `swingbot/admin/helpers.py` (`import_env_text(text) -> tuple[int, list[str]]`), `swingbot/admin/templates/settings.html` (buttons + import modal)
- Test: `tests/admin/test_settings_v2.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: `GET /settings/export` downloads the current `.env` **minus every `sensitive` field entirely** (not masked — omitted, so re-importing an export never silently blanks a real secret), as an attachment `swingbot-settings-<date>.env`. `POST /settings/import` accepts a pasted textarea OR an uploaded file, validates each key against `FIELDS_BY_KEY`, type-checks numerics (skip-on-bad-value rather than corrupt `.env`), and applies known keys via the same `_write_env_text` path `save_settings` itself uses. Sensitive keys ARE applied from an import (pasting a real token is a legitimate use case) even though they're never exported.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

- [ ] **Step 2: Implement**

```python
# swingbot/admin/helpers.py -- add to imports
import io
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/helpers.py

def import_env_text(text: str) -> tuple[int, list[str]]:
    """Parses a pasted/uploaded .env-format text, validates each key
    against FIELDS_BY_KEY, type-checks numerics (a bad numeric value is
    silently skipped rather than corrupting .env), and writes the result
    through the same _write_env_text path save_settings itself uses.
    Sensitive keys ARE applied (a deliberate paste of a real credential is
    a legitimate use case) even though settings_export never emits them.
    Returns (applied_count, unknown_keys)."""
    existing = _read_env_values()
    parsed = dotenv_values(stream=io.StringIO(text))
    applied = 0
    unknown = []
    new_values = dict(existing)
    for key, value in parsed.items():
        if value is None:
            continue
        f = FIELDS_BY_KEY.get(key)
        if f is None:
            unknown.append(key)
            continue
        if f.type in ("number", "float"):
            try:
                float(value)
            except ValueError:
                continue
        new_values[key] = value
        applied += 1

    lines = []
    for section, fields in FIELDS_BY_SECTION:
        lines.append(f"# --- {section} ---")
        for f in fields:
            lines.append(f"{f.key}={new_values.get(f.key, f.default)}")
        lines.append("")
    leftover = {k: v for k, v in new_values.items() if k not in FIELDS_BY_KEY}
    if leftover:
        lines.append("# --- Other / custom variables ---")
        for k, v in leftover.items():
            lines.append(f"{k}={v}")
    _write_env_text("\n".join(lines))
    return applied, unknown
```

```diff
 from .helpers import (
     ...
-    append_settings_audit, read_settings_audit,
+    append_settings_audit, read_settings_audit, import_env_text,
 )
```

```python
# swingbot/admin/app.py

@app.route("/settings/export", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def settings_export():
    existing = _read_env_values()
    lines = []
    for f in config.FIELDS:
        if f.sensitive:
            continue  # omitted entirely, not masked -- an import must never accidentally blank a real secret
        lines.append(f"{f.key}={existing.get(f.key, f.default)}")
    body = "\n".join(lines) + "\n"
    today = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
    return Response(
        body, mimetype="text/plain",
        headers={"Content-Disposition": f"attachment; filename=swingbot-settings-{today}.env"},
    )


@app.route("/settings/import", methods=["POST"])
@require_auth
def settings_import():
    text = request.form.get("env_text", "")
    upload = request.files.get("env_file")
    if upload and upload.filename:
        text = upload.read().decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
    applied_count, unknown_keys = import_env_text(text)
    msg = f"Imported {applied_count} setting(s)."
    if unknown_keys:
        msg += f" Unknown keys skipped: {', '.join(unknown_keys[:10])}."
    return redirect(url_for("settings_page", msg=msg, ok=1))
```

```diff
 {# swingbot/admin/templates/settings.html -- new buttons, right after the
    Recent-changes .card added in C39 #}
+<div class="card">
+  <p class="card-title">Settings profiles</p>
+  <div class="row">
+    <a href="{{ url_for('settings_export') }}" class="secondary small btn" style="text-decoration:none;">⬇ Export .env</a>
+    <button type="button" class="secondary small"
+            onclick="document.getElementById('settings-import-modal').style.display='flex';">⬆ Import .env</button>
```

```diff
 <script>
   function filterSettings() {
     var q = document.getElementById('settings-filter').value.toLowerCase().trim();
+    var onlyChanged = document.getElementById('settings-only-changed').checked;
     document.querySelectorAll('[data-section-card]').forEach(function(card) {
       var anyVisible = false;
       card.querySelectorAll('[data-field-search]').forEach(function(field) {
         var match = !q || field.dataset.fieldSearch.includes(q);
+        if (match && onlyChanged) { match = !!field.querySelector('.changed-dot'); }
         field.style.display = match ? '' : 'none';
         if (match) anyVisible = true;
       });
       card.style.display = anyVisible ? '' : 'none';
     });
   }
+
+  document.querySelectorAll('.reset-field-btn').forEach(function (btn) {
+    btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
+      var target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
+      if (target) { target.value = btn.dataset.default; }
+    });
+  });
 </script>
```

### Task C43: Lifecycle strip + equity sparkline on dashboard

**Files:** Modify `swingbot/admin/app.py` (`_render_dashboard_fragment`, fragment context — the very end of the function, right before its `return render_template(...)` call), `swingbot/admin/templates/dashboard_fragment.html` (stat-row section, lines 54–170)
- Test: `tests/admin/test_dashboard_v2.py`

**Interfaces:**
- Produces: the C15 lifecycle strip (linked to `/plans?status=`) rendered above the existing stat cards; a new "Equity (30d)" stat card embedding `_sparkline_svg` (imported from `pages.py`) over the snapshot's equity-curve last 30 points, with the current account balance as the headline number.
- **Import-order note**: `pages.py` does `from .app import _render, require_auth` at its own top, so `app.py` cannot import `pages.py` at module level without deadlocking on the circular reference (same reasoning as the blueprint registration in C4/C5). `_render_dashboard_fragment` therefore imports `_plan_rows`/`_sparkline_svg` **locally, inside the function body** — by the time this function is actually *called* (request time), both modules are already fully loaded, so the local import is instant and side-effect-free. `analytics.snapshots.load_snapshot`/`refresh_snapshot` have no such circularity and are imported at the top of `app.py` as usual.

- [ ] **Step 1: Failing test**

```python
# tests/admin/test_dashboard_v2.py (append)

def test_dashboard_fragment_shows_lifecycle_strip_and_equity_sparkline(client, auth, admin_app, monkeypatch):
    fake_snapshot = {
        "built_at": "x",
        "equity_curve": [{"ts": f"2026-06-{i + 1:02d}", "balance": 10000 + i * 10} for i in range(30)],
    }
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.app.load_snapshot", lambda max_age_seconds=3600: fake_snapshot)
    monkeypatch.setattr("swingbot.admin.pages.rank_plans", lambda plans: [])
    r = client.get("/dashboard/fragment", headers=auth)
    html = r.data.decode("utf-8")
    assert "lifecycle-strip" in html
    assert "<svg" in html
```

Run: `python -m pytest tests/admin/test_dashboard_v2.py -k equity_sparkline -v`
Expected: FAIL — neither the strip nor the `<svg>` exists in the fragment yet.


```diff

+    # would deadlock. Both modules are fully loaded by request time.
+    from .pages import _plan_rows, _sparkline_svg
+

+    snap = load_snapshot(max_age_seconds=3600) or refresh_snapshot()
+    equity_curve = (snap or {}).get("equity_curve", [])
+    equity_points = [pt["balance"] for pt in equity_curve[-30:]] if equity_curve else []
+    equity_sparkline_svg = _sparkline_svg(equity_points, ref=None) if equity_points else "&mdash;"

     return render_template(
```

- [ ] **Step 3: `stats_page` context (`app.py`, replacing lines 1095–1102)**

```python
@app.route("/performance", methods=["GET"])
@require_auth
def stats_page():
    tl = _trades()
    stats = tl.get_detailed_stats()
    chart_data_json = json.dumps(tl.get_chart_data())

    snap = load_snapshot(max_age_seconds=3600) or refresh_snapshot()
    calibration = (snap or {}).get("calibration", {})
    calibration_chart_json = json.dumps({"deciles": calibration.get("deciles", [])})

    # Local import -- same circularity reasoning as C43 (pages.py imports
    # FROM app.py at its own top).
    from .pages import _heatmap_color, _strategy_horizon_heatmap
    heatmap = _strategy_horizon_heatmap()

    return _render(
        "Performance", "stats", "stats.html", stats=stats, chart_data_json=chart_data_json,
        tiers=calibration.get("tiers", []), drift=calibration.get("drift", []),
        heatmap=heatmap, heatmap_color=_heatmap_color, calibration_chart_json=calibration_chart_json,
    )
```

```diff
+      </td>
+      <td>{% if d.decayed %}<span class="chip chip-decay">DECAY</span>{% else %}—{% endif %}</td>
+    </tr>
+    {% endfor %}
+    </tbody>
+  </table>
+</div>
+
+{% include "_heatmap.html" %}
```

```diff
 {# swingbot/admin/templates/stats.html -- inside the existing bottom-of-file
    <script> block (after Chart.defaults setup, around line 777), render the
    new calibration chart the same way C25's calibration.html does #}
+new Chart(document.getElementById('chart-calibration-deciles'), {
+  type: 'bar',
+  data: (function () {
+    var cal = JSON.parse(document.getElementById('calibration-chart-data').textContent);
+    var deciles = cal.deciles || [];
+    return {
+      labels: deciles.map(function (d) { return 'D' + d.decile; }),
+      datasets: [{
+        label: 'Realized win rate %',
+        data: deciles.map(function (d) { return d.win_rate; }),
+        backgroundColor: deciles.map(function (d) { return d.win_rate >= 80 ? 'rgba(109,218,158,.75)' : 'rgba(226,178,90,.75)'; }),
+      }],
+    };
+  })(),
+  options: {
+    responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
+    plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
+    scales: {
+      y: { min: 0, max: 100, grid: { color: chartDefaults.gridColor }, ticks: { color: chartDefaults.tickColor } },
+      x: { grid: { color: chartDefaults.gridColor }, ticks: { color: chartDefaults.tickColor } },
+    },
+  },
+});
```
